class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367075_comment'></div>俱沾雨露。常谓老死林薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367075_comment'></div>不识阙庭。岂期岩穴久空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367075_comment'></div>弓旌未已。贤才毕用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367075_comment'></div>搜访仍勤。见尧舜之为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367075_comment'></div>追赴上京。曾未浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367075_comment'></div>又拜臣职。顾惭虚受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367075_comment'></div>实惧旷官。捧日无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367075_comment'></div>戴天何报。臣已于正衙辞讫。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　有诗送李宓征南诏。对杨国忠有谀词，对征南诏之举颇为颂扬。作品：《李云南征蛮诗》<div id='poem_45558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45558")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_45558_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_45558'>天宝十一载。有诏伐西南夷。右相杨公兼节制之寄。乃奏前云南守李宓涉海自交趾击之。道路险艰。往复数万里。盖百王所未通也。十二载四月。至于长安。君子是以知庙堂使能。而李公效节。适忝斯人之旧。因赋是诗。</div><div id='poem_preface_45558_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' -----title
商丘（宋城）

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=721&endYear=721')">721年</a>　自长安回宋州，有诗赠友人。作品：《酬庞十兵曹》《别韦参军》<div id='poem_45717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45717' class='poemTitle class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45717'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1210, "poem_allusion_45717")'>邹枚</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45717'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45717'>忆昔游京华，自言生羽翼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45717'>怀书访知己，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_45717", 45717, id='poem_sentence_2_45717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45717'>托身从𤱶亩，浪迹初自得。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45717'>雨泽感天时，耕耘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_45717", 45717, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>忘帝力</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45717'>同人洛阳至，问我睢水北。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45717'>遂尔款津涯，净然见胸臆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45717'>高谈悬物象，逸韵投翰墨。<div gray;'>▪</span>自幽州返宋州，秋，有诗。作品：《送蔡十二之海上》<div id='poem_45535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送蔡十二之海上<span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45535'>黯然何所为，相对但悲酸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45535'>季弟念离别，贤兄救急难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45535'>河流冰处尽，海路雪中寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　回睢阳，李邕遣人送文来，有诗和之。作品：《奉和李泰和<鹘赋>》<div id='poem_1367073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和李泰和鹘赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（743年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367073")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367073_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367073'>天宝初。有自滑台奉太守李公鹘赋以垂示。适越在草野。才无能为。尚怀知音。遂作鹘赋。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367073'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367073'>夫何鹘之为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367073_comment'></div>置之则已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367073_comment'></div>纵之无匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367073_comment'></div>怀果断之沈潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367073_comment'></div>任情性之敏疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367073_comment'></div>头小而锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367073_comment'></div>气雄而逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367073_comment'></div>貌耿介以凌霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367073_comment'></div>目精明而点漆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367073_comment'></div>想像辽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367073_comment'></div>孤贞深密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367073_comment'></div>将必取而乃回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367073_comment'></div>若受词而无失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367073_comment'></div>当白帝之用事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367073_comment'></div>下青霄而委质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367073_comment'></div>乃顺节而勃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367073_comment'></div>因指纵而挺出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367073_comment'></div>严冬欲雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367073_comment'></div>蔓草初焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367073_comment'></div>野莽荡而风紧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367073_comment'></div>天峥嵘而日曛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367073_comment'></div>忿顽兔之狡伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367073_comment'></div>耻高鸟之成群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367073_comment'></div>始灭没而略地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367073_comment'></div>忽升腾而彗云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367073_comment'></div>翻决裂以电击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367073_comment'></div>皆披靡而星分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367073_comment'></div>奔走者折胁而绝脰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367073_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>鸣噪</span>者血洒而毛纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367073_comment'></div>虽百中而自我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367073_comment'></div>终一呼而在君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367073_comment'></div>夫其左右更进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367073_comment'></div>纵横发迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367073_comment'></div>埽窟穴之凌兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367073_comment'></div>振荆榛之淅沥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367073_comment'></div>翕六翮以直上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367073_comment'></div>交双指以迅击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367073_comment'></div>合连弩之应机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367073_comment'></div>类鸣𩩉之破的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367073_comment'></div>豁尔胸臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367073_comment'></div>伊何凌厉以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>爽朗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367073_comment'></div>曾莫虿芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367073_comment'></div>岂虞夷险之怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367073_comment'></div>观其获多不有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367073_comment'></div>得用非媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367073_comment'></div>历阊阖以肃穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367073_comment'></div>翊钩陈以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>环回</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367073_comment'></div>幸耀光于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>蒐狩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367073_comment'></div>承剪拂于楼台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367073_comment'></div>望<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>凤沼</span>而轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367073_comment'></div>纷羽族以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>惊猜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367073_comment'></div>路杳杳而何向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367073_comment'></div>云茫茫而不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367073_comment'></div>莺出谷而徒尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367073_comment'></div>鹤乘轩而何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367073_comment'></div>彼怀毅勇轗轲而弃置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367073_comment'></div>胡不效其閒关而徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367073_comment'></div>尔乃顾恩有地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367073_comment'></div>恋主多情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367073_comment'></div>念层空而不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367073_comment'></div>托虚室而无惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367073_comment'></div>雅节表于能让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367073_comment'></div>义心激于效诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367073_comment'></div>势愈高而下急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367073_comment'></div>体弥重而飞轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367073_comment'></div>戢羽翼以受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367073_comment'></div>若肝胆之必呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367073_comment'></div>嗟日月之云迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367073_comment'></div>犹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>羁縻</span>而见婴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367073_comment'></div>别有横大海而径度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367073_comment'></div>顺长风而一写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367073_comment'></div>投足眇于岩巅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367073_comment'></div>脱身逸于弋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367073_comment'></div>冰落落以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>凝闭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367073_comment'></div>雪皑皑而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1367073", 1367073, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>飘洒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367073_comment'></div>谅坚锐之时然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367073_comment'></div>宁苦寒以求舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367073_comment'></div>匪聚食以祈满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367073_comment'></div>聊击群以自假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367073_comment'></div>比元豹之潜形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367073_comment'></div>同幽人之在野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367073_comment'></div>矧其升巢绝壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367073_comment'></div>独立危条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367073_comment'></div>心倏忽于万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367073_comment'></div>思超遥于九霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367073_comment'></div>岂外物之能慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367073_comment'></div>曷凡禽之见邀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367073_comment'></div>未知鸳鹭之所以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367073_comment'></div>孰与夫鹏鴳之逍遥云尔哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1367073_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=743&endYear=743')">743年</a>　在睢阳，秋冬之交，有诗赠别友人。作品：《宋中遇林虑杨十七山人因而有别》<div id='poem_45649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>画马篇<span class='inlineComment2'>（同诸公宴睢阳李太守，各赋一物。）</span></a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45663'>君侯枥上骢，貌在丹青中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45663'>马毛连钱蹄铁色，图画光辉骄玉勒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45663'>感兹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45663", 45663, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>绝代</span>称<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45663", 45663, "Clauses/6/Comments/1")'>妙手</span>，遂令谈者不容口。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45663'>麒麟独步自可珍，驽骀万匹知何有，终未如他枥上骢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45663'>载华毂，聘飞鸿，荷君剪拂与君用，一日千里如旋风。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_45663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_45655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>遇崔二有别</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45700'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45700'>大国多任士，明时遗此人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45700'>颐颔尚丰盈，毛骨未合迍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45700'>逸足望千里，商歌悲四邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45700'>谁谓多才富，却令家道贫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45700'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_45700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_45700'><span class='label'>按：</span>《适集》卷一有「效古赠崔二」，应是一人。《赠崔二》有云：「君负纵横才，如何尚憔悴。」又云：「穷达自有时，夫子莫下泪。」这次「遇崔二」，还是「明时遗此人」，所以还叹息着说「谁谓多才富，却令家道贫！」<br /></div><div id='poem_note_45700_comment'></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　自扬州至洛阳，过宋州，有文祭张巡、许远。作品：《还京次睢阳父祭张巡许远文》<div id='poem_1367092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1367092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367092'>维乾元元年五月日。太子詹事御史中丞高适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367092_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。敬祭于故御史中丞张许二公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367092_comment'></div>中丞体质贞正。才掩群豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367092_comment'></div>诗书自负。州县徒劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367092_comment'></div>惆怅雄笔。辛勤宝刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367092_comment'></div>时平位下。世乱节高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367092_comment'></div>贼臣通逆。国步惊骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367092_comment'></div>两河震恐。千里嗷嗷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367092_comment'></div>投袂洒泣。据鞍郁陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367092_comment'></div>全谯入宋。收梓捍曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367092_comment'></div>心系魏阙。志清武牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367092_comment'></div>帝曰嗟尔。龙光豹韬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367092_comment'></div>宪台戎幕。持斧拥旄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367092_comment'></div>呜呼。予亦忝窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367092_comment'></div>统兹介冑。俄奉短书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367092_comment'></div>至夔狂寇。裹粮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1367092", 1367092, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>训卒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367092_comment'></div>达曙通昼。军乃促程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367092_comment'></div>书亦封奏。遂发趫勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367092_comment'></div>俾驱鸟兽。将无止心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367092_comment'></div>兵亦死斗。贼党频蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367092_comment'></div>我师旋漏。十城相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367092_comment'></div>百里不救。纭纭啸聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367092_comment'></div>兵锋亦凑。积薪为梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367092_comment'></div>决岸成窦。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367092_comment'></div>当此虎敌。岂无强邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367092_comment'></div>常时肝胆。今日越秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367092_comment'></div>坚守半岁。绝粮数旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367092_comment'></div>柹椽秣马。煮纸饲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367092_comment'></div>病不暇拯。殁无全身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367092_comment'></div>煎熬甲冑。啄啮胶筋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367092_comment'></div>慷慨艰险。凄凉苦辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367092_comment'></div>呜呼。我辞淮楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367092_comment'></div>将赴伊洛。途出兹邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367092_comment'></div>悲缠旧郭。邑里灰烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367092_comment'></div>城池墟落。何九拒之峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367092_comment'></div>皆二贤之制作。声盖天壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367092_comment'></div>气横辽廓。让死争先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367092_comment'></div>临危靡却。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367092_comment'></div>□天亦难论。万夫开壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367092_comment'></div>一旅才存。衰羸既竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367092_comment'></div>力弱相吞。陷阱织路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367092_comment'></div>梯冲栈门。土壕水合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367092_comment'></div>木栅云屯。居即其敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367092_comment'></div>突无其奔。烟云剑戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367092_comment'></div>逼侧纷昏。与求生而害义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367092_comment'></div>宁抗节以埋魂。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367092_comment'></div>悖逆歼溃。干戈将止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367092_comment'></div>海岳澄清。朝廷郅理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367092_comment'></div>封功列爵。怀黄拖紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367092_comment'></div>伤哉二贤。不预于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367092_comment'></div>呜呼孀妇。伶俜爱子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367092_comment'></div>追赠方荣。赏延兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367092_comment'></div>寂寂梁苑。悠悠睢水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367092_comment'></div>黄蒿连接。白骨填委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367092_comment'></div>思壮志于冥寞。问<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1367092", 1367092, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>遗形</span>于荆杞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367092_comment'></div>列祭空城。一悲永矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367092_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1367092_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

北京（范阳）

id='poem_sentence_1_45520'>远行今若此，微禄果徒劳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45520'>绝坂水连下，群峰云共高。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45520'>自堪成白首，何事一青袍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45520'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_45520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬，送兵清夷后回蓟门过年。有诗记送兵事。作品：《送兵到蓟北》<div id='poem_45484' id='poem_sentence_1_45711'>边城何<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作高）</span>萧条，白日黄云昏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45711'>一到征战处，每愁胡虏翻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45711'>岂无安边书，诸将已承恩。<div -----title
易县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='56bf93cef49b408883b2703817944d01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("56bf93cef49b408883b2703817944d01");'><span id='56bf93cef49b408883b2703817944d01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>，35岁</div><div id='56bf93cef49b408883b2703817944d01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　自幽州返宋州，一路漫游，过易县。有诗。作品：《同朱五题卢使君义井》<div id='poem_45553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同朱五题卢使君义井</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45553")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_45553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45553'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45553'>高义唯良牧，深仁自下车。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45553'>宁知凿井处，还是饮冰馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45553'>地即泉源久，人当汲引初。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45553'>体清能鉴物，色洞<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作谈）</span>每<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45553", 45553, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>含虚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45553'>上善滋来往，中和浃里闾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45553'>济时应未竭，怀惠复何如。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45553'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_45553_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

正定（真定）

id='poem_sentence_12_45568'>始佩仙郎印，俄兼太守符。<div id='poem_sentence_12_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_45568'>尤多蜀郡理，更得<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_14_45568'>城邑推雄镇，山川列简图。<div id='poem_sentence_14_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_45568'>旧燕当绝漠，全赵对平芜。<div id='poem_sentence_15_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_45568'>旷野何㳽漫，长亭复郁纡。<div id='poem_sentence_16_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_45568'>始泉遗俗近，活水战场无。<div id='poem_sentence_17_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_45568'>月换思<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_45568", 45568, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>乡陌</span>，星回记<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_45568", 45568, id='poem_sentence_19_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_45568'>沦落而谁遇，栖遑有是夫。<div id='poem_sentence_20_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_45568'>不才羞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_45568", 45568, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>拥肿</span>，干禄谢侏儒。<div id='poem_sentence_26_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_45568'>从来贵缝掖，应是念穷途。<div id='poem_sentence_27_45568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 涉县

"poem_allusion_45588")'>信陵</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45588'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45588'>古城莽苍<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作苍茫）</span>饶荆榛，驱马荒城愁杀人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45588'>魏王<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_1_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45588'>忆昨雄都旧朝市，轩车照耀歌钟起。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45588'>军容带甲三十万，国步连营<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作衡）</span>一<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作五）</span>千里。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45588_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45588'>暮天摇落伤怀抱，倚剑悲歌对秋草。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45588'>侠客犹传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_45588", 45588, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>朱亥</span>名，行人尚识<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(528, "poem_sentence_7_45588")'>夷门</span>道。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45588'>白璧黄金万户侯，宝刀骏马填山丘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45588'>年代凄凉不可问，往来唯有水东流。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
洛阳

id='poem_sentence_7_45722'>我来荐蘋蘩，感叹兴此词。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45722'>晨光上阶闼，杀气翻旌旗。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45722'>明明幽冥理，至诚信莫欺。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45722'>唯夫二千石，多庆方自兹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45722'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_45722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>旅游相州，秋，游铜雀台，有诗。作品：《铜雀妓》<span class='inlineComment2'>（T76，此诗一说作者为王适。）</span><div id='poem_8884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>相和歌辞 铜雀妓<span id='poem_content_8884'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8884'>日暮铜雀迥，幽声<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作深）</span>玉座清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8884'>萧森松柏望，委郁绮罗情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8884'>君恩不再重<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作得）</span>，妾舞为谁轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8884'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_8884_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=742&endYear=742')">742年</a>　寓居淇上，春，有诗记田家生活。作品：《田家春望》<div id='poem_45476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_45624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45624'>孟夏桑叶肥，秾阴<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作濛濛）</span>夹长津。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45624'>蚕农有时节，田野无闲人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45624'>谁能去京洛，憔悴对风尘<span class='inlineComment2'>（自孟夏以下，《英华》作一首）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=742&endYear=742')">742年</a>　在滑州，有诗。寓居淇上，冬，访友，有诗。作品：《渔父歌》<div id='poem_45693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
单县（单父）
-----detail

id='poem_preface_45660'>甲申岁，适登子贱琴台，赋诗三首。首章怀宓公之德，千祀不朽；次章美太守李公，能嗣子贱之政，再造琴台；末章多邑宰崔公，能继子贱之理。</div><div id='poem_preface_45660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45660'><div class='inlineComment2'>（一作清英）</span>，肮脏乃天资。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45645'>方寸且无间，衣冠当在斯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45645'>俱为千里游，忽<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作勿）</span>念两乡辞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45645'>且见壮心在，莫嗟携手迟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45645'>凉风吹北原，落日满<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作照）</span>西陂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45645'>露下草初白，天长云屡滋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45645'>我心不可问<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作得）</span>，君去<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作兮）</span>定何之。<div id='poem_sentence_11_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_45645'>京洛多知己，谁能忆<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(11059, "poem_sentence_12_45645")'>左思</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_45645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_45645'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_45645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋末，离梁宋东征，与李白，杜甫分别。高、李于睢阳分手后，又于单父相遇，纵游甚欢。高杜亦似一路分合数次。自此之东，则三人又分手矣。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
涟水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='da51f39fe65c40f0842bda72a47019ca_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("da51f39fe65c40f0842bda72a47019ca");'><span id='da51f39fe65c40f0842bda72a47019ca_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>，46岁</div><div id='da51f39fe65c40f0842bda72a47019ca' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>由单父经谯郡、彭城、垓下、盱眙、淮阴、山阳等地至襄贲，襄贲即涟水。寓居樊姓地主家。有《东征赋》记行。<div id='poem_1367074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东征赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367074")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367074'>岁在甲申。秋穷季月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367074_comment'></div>高子游梁复久。方适楚以超忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367074_comment'></div>望君门之悠哉。微先容以效拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367074_comment'></div>姑不隐而不仕。宜漂沦而播越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367074_comment'></div>出东苑而遂行。沿浊河而兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367074_comment'></div>感隋皇之败德。划平原而为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367074_comment'></div>西驰洛汭。东并淮涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367074_comment'></div>地豁山开。川流波委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367074_comment'></div>六宫景从。千官逦迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367074_comment'></div>龙舟锦帆。照耀乎数千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367074_comment'></div>大驾将去。群盗日起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367074_comment'></div>尸位者卷舌而偷生。直谏者解颐而后死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367074_comment'></div>寄腹心于枭獍。任手足于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>蛇虺</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367074_comment'></div>既垂弑于匹夫。尚兴疑于爱子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367074_comment'></div>岂不为穷力役于征战。务淫逸于奢侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367074_comment'></div>六军悲牧野之师。万姓哭辽阳之鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367074_comment'></div>嗟颠覆于曩日。指年代于流水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367074_comment'></div>唯见长亭之烟火。悲旷野之荆杞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367074_comment'></div>至酂县之旧邑。怀萧相之高风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367074_comment'></div>既屈节于主吏。每归诚于沛公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367074_comment'></div>始俱起于天下。乃从定于关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367074_comment'></div>推金帛于他人。挹图籍于我躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367074_comment'></div>按山川之险阻。救天地于屯蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367074_comment'></div>嘉盈俸以增邑。方指纵而建功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367074_comment'></div>纳邵平以防患。举曹参而告终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367074_comment'></div>经洛城而永望。想谯郡而销忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367074_comment'></div>慨魏武之雄图。终大济于横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367074_comment'></div>用兵戈以威四海。挟天子而令诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367074_comment'></div>乃擅命以诛伏。徒矫迹以安刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367074_comment'></div>吾始未知夫逆顺。胡宁比于殷周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367074_comment'></div>下符离之西偏。临彭城之高岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367074_comment'></div>连山郁其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>漭荡</span>。分大泽乎渺漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367074_comment'></div>忆昔天未厌祸。项氏叛涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367074_comment'></div>解齐归楚。自萧击汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367074_comment'></div>天地无色。风云<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>溃乱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367074_comment'></div>悯君王之坎轲。混士卒以奔散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367074_comment'></div>苟炎运之克昌。岂人生之涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367074_comment'></div>次灵壁之逆旅。面垓下之遗墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367074_comment'></div>嗟鲁公之慷慨。闻楚声而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>悒于</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367074_comment'></div>歌拔山以涕洟。窃霸图而莫居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367074_comment'></div>摈亚父之何甚。悲虞姬之有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367074_comment'></div>出重围而狼狈。至阴陵以踌躇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367074_comment'></div>顾天亡以自负。虽身死兮焉如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367074_comment'></div>登夏邱以寓目。对蒲隧而愁予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367074_comment'></div>闻取虑之斯在。微长直而舍诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367074_comment'></div>宿徐县之回津。惟偃王之旧域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367074_comment'></div>方以小而事大。岂无位而有德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367074_comment'></div>彼皆昏暴以丧邦。伊何仁义而亡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367074_comment'></div>高延陵之挂剑。慕班彪之述职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367074_comment'></div>缅沛水之悠悠。俯娄林之纡直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367074_comment'></div>即日河浒。依然泗上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367074_comment'></div>山川土地。耳目清旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367074_comment'></div>眺睢源之呀豁。倚楚关之雄壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367074_comment'></div>挂轻席于中流。顺长风以破浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367074_comment'></div>过盱眙之邑屋。伤义帝之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>波荡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367074_comment'></div>叹三户之亡秦。知万人以离项。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367074_comment'></div>越龟山而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>访泊</span>。入渔浦而待潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367074_comment'></div>鸿雁飞兮木叶下。楚歌悲兮雨潇潇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367074_comment'></div>霜封野树。冰冻寒苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367074_comment'></div>岸草无色。芦花自飘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367074_comment'></div>幸息肩于人事。愿投迹于渔樵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367074_comment'></div>思魏阙而天远。向秦川而路遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367074_comment'></div>候鸣鸡以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>进帆</span>。趋乱流以争迅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367074_comment'></div>纵孤舟于浩大。抚垂堂以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>诫慎</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367074_comment'></div>遵枉渚于淮阴。徵昔贤于韩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367074_comment'></div>哀王孙之寄食。嘉漂母之无愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367074_comment'></div>鄙亭长之不仁。乃晨炊而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1367074", 1367074, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>啬吝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367074_comment'></div>忽从龙以获骋。遂擒豹以自奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367074_comment'></div>破全赵有奇谋。称假齐以益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367074_comment'></div>幸辞通以感惠。俄结豨而谋衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367074_comment'></div>当处约而心亨。曷持盈而不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367074_comment'></div>陵赤岸之迢递。棹白浪之纡馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367074_comment'></div>历山阳之村野。投襄贲之邑居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367074_comment'></div>人多耆艾。俗喜观渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367074_comment'></div>连葭苇于郊甸。杂汀洲于里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367074_comment'></div>感百川之朝宗。弥结念于归欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367074_comment'></div>日杲杲以丽天。云飘飘以卷舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367074_comment'></div>鲁放情而蹈海。孔永叹于乘桴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367074_comment'></div>遇坎则止。吾今不知其所如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367074_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1367074_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>居涟水，有诗赠别友人。作品：《涟上别王秀才》<div id='poem_45686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涟上别王秀才</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45686")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45686'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45686'>飘飖经远道，客思满穷秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45686'>浩荡对长涟，君行殊未休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45686'>崎岖山海侧，想像无前俦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45686'>何意<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岂谓）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45686", 45686, "Clauses/6/Comments/1")'>照乘珠</span>，忽然欲暗投。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45686'>东路方萧条，楚歌复悲愁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45686'>暮帆使人感，去鸟兼离忧。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45686'>行矣当自爱，壮年莫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_45686", 45686, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>悠悠</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45686'>余亦从此辞，异乡难久留。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45686'>赠言岂终极，慎勿滞沧洲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45686'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_45686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>居涟水，寓樊家，有诗题樊氏水亭。作品：《涟上题樊氏水亭》<div id='poem_45687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涟上题樊氏水亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45687")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45687'>涟上非所趣，偶为世务牵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45687'>经时驻归棹，日夕对平川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45687'>莫论行子愁，且得主人贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45687'>亭上酒初熟，厨中鱼每鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45687'>自说宦游来，因之居住偏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45687'>煮盐沧海曲，种稻长淮边。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45687'>四时常晏如，百口无饥年。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45687'>菱芋藩篱下，渔樵耳目前。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45687'>异县少朋从，我行复迍邅。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45687'>向不逢此君，孤舟已言旋。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45687'>明日又分首<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作手）</span>，风涛还眇然。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45687'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_45687_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
东平（须昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='40cddcec037c46b8b12bc49fbc1f306f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("40cddcec037c46b8b12bc49fbc1f306f");'><span id='40cddcec037c46b8b12bc49fbc1f306f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>，46岁</div><div id='40cddcec037c46b8b12bc49fbc1f306f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=745&endYear=745')">745年</a>　由涟水经泗水西北行，至东平，有诗纪行。作品：《鲁西至东平》<div id='poem_45701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲁西至东平</a><span class='authorDate'>（745年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45701")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45701_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45701'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1329, "poem_allusion_45701")'>问津</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2427, "poem_allusion_45701")'>家丘</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45701'>沙岸拍不定，石桥水横流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45701'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1329, "poem_sentence_1_45701")'>问津</span>见鲁俗<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作叟）</span>，怀古伤<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2427, "poem_sentence_1_45701")'>家丘</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45550'>御史风逾劲，郎官草屡修。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45550'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_45550", 45550, "Clauses/10/Comments/1")'>鹓鸾</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2950, "poem_sentence_5_45550")'>粉署</span>起，鹰隼<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(420, "poem_sentence_5_45550")'>柏台</span>秋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45550'>出入交三事，飞鸣揖<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8945, "poem_sentence_6_45550")'>五侯</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45550'>军书陈上策，廷议借前筹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45550'>肃肃趋朝列，雍雍引帝求。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45550'>一麾俄出守，千里再分忧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45550'>不改<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(211, "poem_sentence_10_45550")'>任棠水</span>，仍传<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9607, "poem_sentence_10_45550")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_45550", 45550, "Clauses/21/Comments/1")'>晏子裘</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45550'>歌谣随举扇，旌旆逐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_45550", 45550, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>鸣驺</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_45550'>郡国长河绕，川原大野幽。<div id='poem_sentence_12_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_45550'>地连尧泰岳，山向禹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_45550", 45550, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>青州</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_45550'>汶上春帆渡，秦亭晚日愁。<div id='poem_sentence_14_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_45550'>遗墟当少昊，悬象逼奎娄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_45550'>即此逢清鉴，终然喜暗投。<div id='poem_sentence_16_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_45550'>叨承<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1463, "poem_sentence_17_45550")'>解榻</span>礼，更得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_45550", 45550, "Clauses/35/Comments/1")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8810, "poem_sentence_17_45550")'>问缣</span>游</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_45550'>高兴陪登陟，嘉言忝献酬。<div id='poem_sentence_18_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_45550'>观棋知战胜，探象会冥搜。<div id='poem_sentence_19_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_45550'>眺听情何限，冲融惠勿休。<div id='poem_sentence_20_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_45550'>祗应齐语默，宁肯问沈浮。<div id='poem_sentence_21_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_45550'>然诺长怀季，栖遑辄累丘。<div id='poem_sentence_22_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_45550'>平生感知己，方寸岂悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_23_45550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_45550'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_45550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，在东平，有文。作品：《为东平薛太守进王氏瑞诗表》<div id='poem_1367083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为东平薛太守进王氏瑞诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367083")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367083'>臣某言。符瑞之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367083_comment'></div>实由王政。歌诗之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367083_comment'></div>本自国风。伏见范阳卢某母琅琊王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367083_comment'></div>性合希夷。体于静默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367083_comment'></div>精微道本。驰骛元关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367083_comment'></div>旁通天地之心。豫纪休徵之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367083_comment'></div>去景龙二载。撰天宝回文诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367083_comment'></div>凡八百一十二字。循环有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367083_comment'></div>若寒暑之递迁。应变无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367083_comment'></div>谓阴阳之莫测。诫其子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367083_comment'></div>吾没之后。尔密记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367083_comment'></div>当逢大道之朝。必遇非常之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367083_comment'></div>则真图之制。便可上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367083_comment'></div>君亲之义不违。犬马之诚斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367083_comment'></div>臣早识其子。常与臣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367083_comment'></div>星霜屡移。书奏仍阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367083_comment'></div>以岁月悠远。旨趣幽微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367083_comment'></div>沈吟取耳目之前。倏忽应祯祥之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367083_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下乘道御极。至圣兴化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367083_comment'></div>参日月之并明。一乾坤而同德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367083_comment'></div>梯航万里。争饮淳和之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367083_comment'></div>臣妾四夷。尽归仁寿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367083_comment'></div>今陛下务于道。道可尽乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367083_comment'></div>法于天。天实长久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367083_comment'></div>是知与道齐运。比天同休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367083_comment'></div>无疆之休。乃在兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367083_comment'></div>则王氏之美。其可替乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367083_comment'></div>章句粲然。所谓没而不朽者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367083_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。昔汉幸甘泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367083_comment'></div>且昧神君之语。周穷辙迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367083_comment'></div>徒称王母之谣。岂若迥出名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367083_comment'></div>高悬响像。应皇王之丕命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367083_comment'></div>运宫商于景福。且夫灵芝嘉禾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367083_comment'></div>草木之瑞者。黄龙丹雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367083_comment'></div>禽兽之瑞者。犹能光扬帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367083_comment'></div>标榜颂声。方之真图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367083_comment'></div>彼未为得。特望编之史策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367083_comment'></div>列在乐章。则陛下先于天而听于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367083_comment'></div>臣才术浅劣。谬忝藩垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367083_comment'></div>曾微涓尘。以答万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367083_comment'></div>恒驰北极。每切子牟之恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367083_comment'></div>遥奉南山。愿效封人之祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367083_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1367083_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
济南（历城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='02de508756394620a7b75b59733446bc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("02de508756394620a7b75b59733446bc");'><span id='02de508756394620a7b75b59733446bc_link' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45500")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_45500_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45500'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2269, "poem_allusion_45500")'>李郭舟</span>　<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_1_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45670'>秪言小邑无所为，公门百事皆有期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45670'>归<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作悲）</span>来向家问妻子，举家尽笑今如此。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45670'>生事应须南亩田，世情付与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_45670", 45670, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>东流水</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45670'>梦想<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_45670", 45670, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>旧山</span>安在哉，为衔君命且<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作日）</span>迟回。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45670'>乃知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_45670", 45670, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>梅福</span>徒为尔，转忆陶潜归去来。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45670'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_45670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_45670'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(45670)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_45483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>封丘作</a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45483")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_45483_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45483'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3471, "poem_allusion_45483")'>愚公</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45483'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45483'>州县才难适，云山道欲穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45483'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_45483", 45483, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>揣摩</span>惭黠吏，栖隐谢<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3471, "poem_sentence_1_45483")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_45483", 45483, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>愚公</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45483'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_45483_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f84060ae6d1f47c88662e57fee009ee6_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=752')">751-752年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='f84060ae6d1f47c88662e57fee009ee6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>　回封丘，对县尉生活极端不满，秋，有诗赠友人。作品：《同颜六少府旅宦秋中之作》<div id='poem_45506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同颜六少府旅宦秋中之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（748年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45506")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_45506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45506'>传君昨夜怅然悲，独坐新斋木落时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45506'>逸气旧来凌燕雀，高才何得混妍媸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45506'>迹留<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作劳）</span>黄绶人多叹，心在青云世莫知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45506'>不是鬼神无正直，从来州县有瑕疵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45506'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_45506_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年9月</a>　回封丘，九月九日，有诗赠友人。诗中对县尉生活极为不满。作品：《九月九日酬颜少府》<div id='poem_45577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日酬颜少府</a><span class='authorDate'>（749年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45577")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_45577_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45577'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1113, "poem_allusion_45577")'>蔡泽丑</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45577'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45577'>檐前白日应可惜，篱下黄花为谁有。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45577'>行<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作客）</span>子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_45577", 45577, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>迎霜</span>未授衣，主人得钱始<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作肯）</span>沽酒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45577'>苏秦憔悴人<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作时）</span>多厌，蔡泽栖迟<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作栖遑）</span>世看丑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45577'>纵使登高只断肠，不如独坐空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45577", 45577, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>搔首</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45577'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_45577_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>　在封丘，有诗和友人，明白表示不愿再任县尉。作品：《奉酬睢阳路太守见赠之作》<div id='poem_45559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉酬睢阳路太守见赠<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作贻）</span>之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45559")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_45559_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45559'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2263, "poem_allusion_45559")'>登龙</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3388, "poem_allusion_45559")'>刘公干</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9206, "poem_allusion_45559")'>向子期</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45559'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45559'>盛才膺命代，高价动良时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45559'>帝简登藩翰，人和发咏思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45559'>神仙去华省，鹓鹭忆丹墀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45559'>清净能无事，优游即赋诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45559'>江山纷想像，云物共<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作动）</span>萎蕤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45559'>逸气<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3388, "poem_sentence_5_45559")'>刘公干</span>，玄言<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9206, "poem_sentence_5_45559")'>向子期</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45559'>多惭汲引速，翻愧激昂迟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45559'>相马知何限，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2263, "poem_sentence_7_45559")'>登龙</span>反自疑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45559'>风尘吏道迫，行迈旅心悲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45559'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_45559", 45559, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>拙疾</span>徒为尔，穷愁欲问谁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45559'>秋庭一片叶，朝镜数茎丝。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45559'>州县甘无取，丘园悔莫追。<div id='poem_sentence_11_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_45559'>琼瑶生箧笥，光景借茅茨。<div id='poem_sentence_12_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_45559'>他日青霄里，犹应访所知。<div id='poem_sentence_13_45559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_45559'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_45559_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　上半年，仍在封丘任职，有文。作品：《陈留郡上源新驿记》<div id='poem_1367089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈留郡上源新驿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367089")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367089'>周官。行夫掌邦国传遽之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367089_comment'></div>施于政者。盖有章焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367089_comment'></div>皇唐之兴。盛于古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367089_comment'></div>自京师四极。经启十道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367089_comment'></div>道列以亭。亭实以驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367089_comment'></div>而亭惟三十里。驷有上中下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367089_comment'></div>丰屋美食。供亿是为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367089_comment'></div>人迹所穷。帝命流洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367089_comment'></div>用之远者。莫若于斯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367089_comment'></div>伊陈留雄称山东。声英海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367089_comment'></div>昌大嚣庶。有梁魏之遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367089_comment'></div>风烟两河之眇。襟带九州之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367089_comment'></div>洎皇华轺传。夷使骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367089_comment'></div>出关而驰。南向北户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367089_comment'></div>山川水陆之役。兆于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367089_comment'></div>故上源所置。与其难哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367089_comment'></div>居里之冲。濒河之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367089_comment'></div>地形湫隘。馆次卑狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367089_comment'></div>巽在堤下。面于剧旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367089_comment'></div>走庭以隅。建步终坎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367089_comment'></div>车靡方驾。骑无并鞭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367089_comment'></div>其郁闭有如此者。壬辰岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367089_comment'></div>太守元公连率河南之三载也。尧治四岳而神人理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367089_comment'></div>汉诏八使而风俗清。举德推贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367089_comment'></div>事高典策。革已成之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367089_comment'></div>持独断之明。迨兹邮亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367089_comment'></div>俯视颓朽。何逼侧蹇浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367089_comment'></div>不称其声。将图鼎新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367089_comment'></div>岂曰仍旧。顾谓长史李公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367089_comment'></div>夫开释故实。发挥制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367089_comment'></div>不有攸居者。谁其允协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367089_comment'></div>今奏计阙前。先甲而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367089_comment'></div>小大之务。公其领之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367089_comment'></div>申命录事参军冯元掌曰。维操绳墨者盖用于正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367089_comment'></div>蕴廉慎者俾临于财。公以正身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367089_comment'></div>用财均力。纪纲相佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367089_comment'></div>善莫大焉。复命浚仪令裴胜曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367089_comment'></div>公之为县也。易于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367089_comment'></div>训迪其源。秉清白之一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367089_comment'></div>据忠信之馀地。夫忠以创物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367089_comment'></div>清而守官。立言有程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367089_comment'></div>指使而可。于是北吞里室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367089_comment'></div>人以利迁也。南豁路旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367089_comment'></div>事无苟免也。合土以峻墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367089_comment'></div>攻木以高户。栋宇相翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367089_comment'></div>群材如生。兹所谓动乃有经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367089_comment'></div>徐而不费。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367089_comment'></div>久于否者。宜以改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367089_comment'></div>本于功者。终乎永贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367089_comment'></div>则亭之成焉。我方访王公澄清之初也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367089_comment'></div>公时膺迈德。天与大才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367089_comment'></div>属梁宋不登。朝廷旰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367089_comment'></div>求瘼之重。不其然欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367089_comment'></div>用能官去秕政。人无菜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367089_comment'></div>百城偃于迅风。万象纳于明镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367089_comment'></div>乃因寮吏。慨然于兹亭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367089_comment'></div>且夫木石之新者。而犹可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367089_comment'></div>况人而自新。孰不观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367089_comment'></div>又曰。传不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367089_comment'></div>启塞从时。用之善者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367089_comment'></div>而今而后。吾以无事为事焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367089_comment'></div>君子是以知邮亭之可嘉。而我公之清净无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367089_comment'></div>末吏不敏。纪于贞石云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367089_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1367089_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
濮阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0c60a4e9bb3d41efba517de3ba712f1a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0c60a4e9bb3d41efba517de3ba712f1a");'><span id='0c60a4e9bb3d41efba517de3ba712f1a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年</a>，51岁</div><div id='0c60a4e9bb3d41efba517de3ba712f1a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，送兵清夷，途出濮阳，与沈千运相遇。有诗赠之。作品：《赋得<还山吟>送沈四山人》<div id='poem_45698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45698' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45698?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赋得还山吟送沈四山人</a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45698")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45698'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45698'>还山吟，天高日暮寒山深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45698'>送君还山识君心，人生老大须恣意。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45698'>看君解作一生事，山间偃仰无不至。<div -----title
河间
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8fd36be9dc964150ba2821cd3b08053c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8fd36be9dc964150ba2821cd3b08053c");'><span id='8fd36be9dc964150ba2821cd3b08053c_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年</a>　送兵清夷，暂驻河间，与友人泛舟清河。有诗记之。作品：《同敬八卢五泛河间清河》<div id='poem_45600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同敬八卢五汎河间清河</a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45600")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45600'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45600'>清川在城下，沿汎多所宜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45600'>同济惬数公，玩物欣良时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45600'>飘飖波上兴，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_45600", 45600, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>燕婉</span>舟中词。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45600'>昔陟乃平原，今来忽涟漪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45600'>东流达沧海，西流延滹池。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45600'>云树共晦明，井邑相逶迤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45600'>稍随归月帆，若与沙鸥期。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45600'>渔父更留我，前潭水未滋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45600'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_45600_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
定州（安喜）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='135e3d056d944909977d39511eafa24a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("135e3d056d944909977d39511eafa24a");'><span id='135e3d056d944909977d39511eafa24a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年</a>，51岁</div><div id='135e3d056d944909977d39511eafa24a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>送兵清夷，过博陵郡，有诗赠诸友人。作品：《酬秘书弟兼寄幕下诸公》<div id='poem_45718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬秘书弟兼寄幕下诸公</a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45718")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45718_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_45718'>乙亥岁，适徵诣长安，时侍御杨公任通事舍人，诗书起予，盖终日矣。今年适自封丘尉统吏卒于青夷，途经博陵，得太守贾公之政，相见如旧，他日之意存焉。司业张侯，周旋迨兹，仅三十载，将畴昔是好，匪穷达之异乎。族弟秘书，雁序之白眉者，风尘一别。俱东西南北之人，怆然相逢，适与愿契。旅馆之暇，长怀益增，因赋是诗，愧非六义之流也。</div><div id='poem_preface_45718_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45718'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(43, -----title
冀州（信都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4728d483ac2c40e588b6121754ad1a0a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4728d483ac2c40e588b6121754ad1a0a");'><span id='4728d483ac2c40e588b6121754ad1a0a_link' id='poem_sentence_0_45697'>常日好读书，晚年学垂纶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45697'>漆园多乔木，睢水清<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_45697'>诏书下柴门，天命敢逡巡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45697'>赫赫三伏时，十日到咸秦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45697'>褐衣不得见，黄绶翻在身。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45697'>吏道顿羁束，生涯难重陈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45697'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_45697", 45697, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>北使</span>经大寒，关山饶苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45697'>边兵若刍狗，战骨成埃尘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45697'>行矣勿复言，归欤伤我神。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45697'>如何燕赵陲，忽遇平生亲。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45697'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_45697", 45697, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>开馆</span>纳征骑，弹弦娱远宾。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45697'>飘飖天地间，一别方兹晨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_45697'>东道有佳作，南朝无此人。<div id='poem_sentence_12_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_45697'>性灵出万象，风骨超常伦。<div id='poem_sentence_13_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_45697'>吾党谢<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8580, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_45697'>明时取秀才，落日过蒲津。<div id='poem_sentence_15_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_45697'>节苦名已富，禄微家转贫。<div id='poem_sentence_16_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_45697'>相逢愧薄游，抚己荷陶钧。<div id='poem_sentence_17_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_45697'>心事正堪尽，离居<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作忧）</span>宁太频。<div id='poem_sentence_18_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_45697'>两河归路遥，二月芳草新。<div id='poem_sentence_19_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_45697'>柳接滹沱暗，莺连渤海春。<div id='poem_sentence_20_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_45697'>谁谓行路难，猥当希代珍。<div id='poem_sentence_21_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_45697'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_45697", 45697, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>提握</span>每终日，相思犹比邻。<div id='poem_sentence_22_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_45697'>江海有扁舟，丘园有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_45697", 45697, id='poem_sentence_24_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_45697'>浮沈各异宜，老大贵全真。<div id='poem_sentence_25_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_45697'>莫作云霄计，遑遑随缙绅。<div id='poem_sentence_26_45697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_45697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_45697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过信都，有诗咏汉审食其之封地辟阳城。借审食其与吕后事以影射安禄山与杨贵妃之丑闻。作品：《辟阳城》<div id='poem_45575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45575'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45575'>荒城在高岸，凌眺俯清淇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45575'>传道汉天子，而封审食其。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45575'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_45575", 45575, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>奸淫</span>且不戮，茅土孰云宜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45575'>何得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45575", 45575, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>英雄</span>主，返令儿女欺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45575'>母仪良已失，臣节岂如斯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45575'>太息一朝事，乃令人所嗤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45575'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_45575_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
乐都（临洮军）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d49c2969467c4fd28a7856d0edc16bce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d49c2969467c4fd28a7856d0edc16bce");'><span id='d49c2969467c4fd28a7856d0edc16bce_link'
