href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　秋，受田梁丘推荐，赴武威河西幕府谒哥舒翰，不遇；转自临洮陇右，始为入幕之宾。有诗记之。作品：《自武威赴临洮谒大夫不及因书即事寄河西陇右幕下诸公》<div id='poem_45613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自武威赴临洮谒大夫不及因书即事寄河西陇右幕下诸公</a><span class='authorDate'>（753年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45613")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45613'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45613'>浩荡去乡县，飘飖瞻节旄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45613'>扬鞭发武威，落日至临洮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45613'>主人未相识，客子心忉忉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45613'>顾见征战归，始知士马豪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45613'>戈鋋耀崖谷，声气如风涛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45613'>隐轸戎旅间，功业竞相褒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45613'>献状陈首级，飨军烹太牢。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45613'>俘囚驱面缚，长幼随颠毛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45613'>毡裘何蒙茸，血食本膻臊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_45613'>汉将乃儿戏，秦人空自劳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_45613'>立马眺洪河，惊风吹白蒿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_45613'>云屯寒色苦，雪合群山高。<div id='poem_sentence_11_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_45613'>远戍际天末，边烽连贼壕。<div id='poem_sentence_12_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_45613'>我本江海游，逝将心利逃。<div id='poem_sentence_13_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_45613'>一朝感推荐，万里从英髦。<div id='poem_sentence_14_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_45613'>飞鸣盖殊伦，俯仰忝诸曹。<div id='poem_sentence_15_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_45613'>燕颔知有待，龙泉惟所操。<div id='poem_sentence_16_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_45613'>相士惭入幕，怀贤愿同袍。<div id='poem_sentence_17_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_45613'>清抡挥麈尾，乘酣持蟹螯。<div id='poem_sentence_18_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_45613'>此行岂易酬，深意方郁陶。<div id='poem_sentence_19_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_45613'>微效傥不遂，终然辞佩刀。<div id='poem_sentence_20_45613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_45613'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_45613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　在临洮军，有文议董卓庙。作品：《后汉贼臣董卓庙议》<div id='poem_1367086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后汉贼臣董卓庙议</a><span class='authorDate'>（753年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367086")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367086'>昔汉祚陵夷。桓灵弃德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367086_comment'></div>宦官用事。国步多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367086_comment'></div>宗社有缀旒之危。宰臣非补衮之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367086_comment'></div>董卓地兼形胜。手握兵钤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367086_comment'></div>颠而不扶。祸则先唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367086_comment'></div>兴晋阳之甲。君侧未除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367086_comment'></div>入洛阳之宫。臣节如扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367086_comment'></div>至乃发掘园寝。逼辱妃嫔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367086_comment'></div>太后之崩。岂称天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367086_comment'></div>宏农之废。孰谓人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367086_comment'></div>敢讽朝廷。以自尊贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367086_comment'></div>大肆剽虏。以极诛求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367086_comment'></div>焚烧都邑。驰突放横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367086_comment'></div>衣冠冻馁。倚死墙壁之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367086_comment'></div>兆庶困穷。生涂草莽之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367086_comment'></div>于是天地愤怒。鬼神号哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367086_comment'></div>而山东义旗。攘袂争起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367086_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367086", 1367086, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>连州跨郡</span>。皆以诛卓为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367086_comment'></div>故兵挫于孙坚。气夺于袁绍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367086_comment'></div>僭拟舆服。党助奸邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367086_comment'></div>驱蹙东人。胁帝西幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367086_comment'></div>淫刑以逞。有汤镬之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367086_comment'></div>要之糜烂。刳剔异端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367086_comment'></div>乃谓汉鼎可移。郿坞方盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367086_comment'></div>殊不知祸盈恶稔。未或不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367086_comment'></div>故神赞允诚。天假布手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367086_comment'></div>母妻屠戮。种族无留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367086_comment'></div>悬首燃脐。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1367086", 1367086, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>遗臭万代</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367086_comment'></div>骨肉灰烬。不其快哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367086_comment'></div>今狄道之人。不惭卓之不臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367086_comment'></div>而务其为鬼。苟斯鬼足尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367086_comment'></div>则汉莽可得而神。晋敦可得而庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367086_comment'></div>桓元父子。可享于江乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367086_comment'></div>尔朱弟兄。可祀于朔上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367086_comment'></div>嗟乎。仁贤之魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367086_comment'></div>寂寞于邱陵。义烈之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367086_comment'></div>沈埋于泉壤。何馨香之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367086_comment'></div>而用于暴悖之鬼哉。适窃奉吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367086_comment'></div>庇身戎幕。每承馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367086_comment'></div>饱识公忠之言。不远下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367086_comment'></div>尽知仁义之本。昨忝高会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367086_comment'></div>敬受德音。今具贼臣之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367086_comment'></div>悉以条上。谨按尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367086_comment'></div>王者望秩天地之神祇。诸侯祭境内之山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367086_comment'></div>乱臣不言。淫祀无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367086_comment'></div>则董卓之庙。义当焚毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367086_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1367086_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　崇佛，与哥舒翰等造《阿弥陀经》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　哥舒翰表高适为左骁卫兵曹，充掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　在陇右节度幕内，有诗送浑惟明出塞。作品：《送浑将军出塞》<div id='poem_45675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送浑将军出塞</a><span class='authorDate'>（754年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45675")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45675_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_sentence_0_45675'>将军族贵兵且强，汉家已是浑邪王。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45675'>子孙相承在朝野，至今部曲燕支下。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45675'>控弦尽用阴山儿，登<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作临）</span>阵常骑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_45675", 45675, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>大宛马</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　寄诗颜真卿叙旧。作品：《奉寄平原颜太守》<div id='poem_45656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_note_45656_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年7月</a>　与友人游玩，宴会，有诗。作品：《陪窦侍御灵云南亭宴诗得雷字》<div id='poem_45571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪窦侍御灵云南亭宴诗得雷字</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45571")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_45571_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_45571'>凉州近胡，高下其池亭，盖以耀蕃落也。幕府董帅雄勇，径践戎庭，自阳关而西，犹枕席矣。军中无事，君子饮食宴乐，宜哉。白简在边，清秋多兴，况水具舟楫，山兼亭台，始临泛而写烦。俄登陟以寄傲，丝桐徐奏，林木更爽，觞蒲萄以递欢，指兰茝而可掇。胡天一望，云物苍然，雨萧萧而牧马声断，风袅袅而边歌几处，又足悲矣。员外李公曰：七日者何？牛女之夕也。夫贤者何得谨其时，请赋南亭诗，列之于后。</div><div id='poem_preface_45571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45571'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45571'>人幽宜眺听，目极喜亭台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45571'>风景知愁在，关山忆梦回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45571'>秪言殊语默，何意忝游陪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45571'>连唱波澜动，冥搜物象开。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367087_comment'></div>铸海上之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367087_comment'></div>江淮之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367087_comment'></div>盖奔命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367087_comment'></div>岂财赋之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367087_comment'></div>抑以从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367087_comment'></div>将利害之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367087_comment'></div>犹有所阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367087_comment'></div>庙堂精思其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367087_comment'></div>表窦公自宪闱而董之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367087_comment'></div>开释丛脞之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367087_comment'></div>发挥卤莽之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367087_comment'></div>政之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367087_comment'></div>不其然与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367087_comment'></div>今农夫力于必登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367087_comment'></div>廉贾知夫踊贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367087_comment'></div>鸣戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367087_comment'></div>若惟斯之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367087_comment'></div>以见天下之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367087_comment'></div>我幕府凉公勤劳王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367087_comment'></div>常用此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367087_comment'></div>干戈所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367087_comment'></div>戎狄相吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367087_comment'></div>宜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367087_comment'></div>八月既望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367087_comment'></div>公于是领钱谷之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367087_comment'></div>归奏朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367087_comment'></div>副节制郎中裴公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367087_comment'></div>军司马员外李公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367087_comment'></div>追台阁之旧游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367087_comment'></div>惜轩车之远别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367087_comment'></div>席楼船于池上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367087_comment'></div>泛云物于城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367087_comment'></div>胡琴羌笛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367087_comment'></div>缭绕隈隩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367087_comment'></div>舞罗袨装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367087_comment'></div>映带洲渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367087_comment'></div>醉后欢甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367087_comment'></div>东日遐瞻<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作东林日高）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367087_comment'></div>语歧路于樽前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367087_comment'></div>指京华于天杪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367087_comment'></div>有若司直崔公之逸韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367087_comment'></div>嘉其廷评数贤之閒作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367087_comment'></div>适忝斯人之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367087_comment'></div>敢拜首而序云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1367087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　访友人，有诗。作品：《武威同诸公过杨七山人得藤字》<div id='poem_45522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45522' class='poemTitle -----title
凤县（河池）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2d642d40a1c041a8a12416dc3894977c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2d642d40a1c041a8a12416dc3894977c");'><span id='2d642d40a1c041a8a12416dc3894977c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>，57岁</div><div id='2d642d40a1c041a8a12416dc3894977c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年6月9日</a>　玄宗西逃，高适间道追及于河池郡。谒见唐玄宗，分析潼关失败时之形势，极言朝廷军政之腐败。玄宗嘉之，寻迁侍御史。<br /></div>

成都

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年1月</a>　正月，史朝义自缢，安史之乱平。有贺表。作品：《贺收城表》<div id='poem_1367080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺收城表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367080")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367080'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367080'>臣某言。闰正月十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367080_comment'></div>中使郭罗至。伏奉敕书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367080_comment'></div>示臣圣略。收复洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367080_comment'></div>扫殄凶徒。臣某手之足之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367080_comment'></div>载欣载跃。臣闻天不假易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367080_comment'></div>将而必诛。守在四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367080_comment'></div>难逃一面。顷者逆胡稔恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367080_comment'></div>窃据中都。欲驱犬羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367080_comment'></div>敢肆虿毒。碎首于雷霆之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367080_comment'></div>窜迹于城社之中。犹贮残魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367080_comment'></div>拟收馀烬。陛下泽深覆载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367080_comment'></div>功济艰难。神武必止于干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367080_comment'></div>寰区大拯于涂炭。好生恶杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367080_comment'></div>诚屡发于宸心。走兽奔禽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367080_comment'></div>尽已罹于网目。使风云一变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367080_comment'></div>日月增辉。巨海绝其扬波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367080_comment'></div>妖氛化为和气。臣忝司戎律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367080_comment'></div>累奉德音。昭宣睿谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367080_comment'></div>底宁县道。天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367080_comment'></div>岂独方隅。无任庆快之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367080_comment'></div>谨遣洋州司马员外同正员摄参谋臣路球奉表陈贺以闻。臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367080_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1367080_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年2月</a>　就任剑南西川节度使，摄东川节度使。有谢表。作品：《谢上剑南节度使表》<div id='poem_1367077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢上剑南节度使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367077")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367077'>臣某言。受脤登坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367077_comment'></div>必先礼乐。剖符揽辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367077_comment'></div>是委腹心。方将总领诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367077_comment'></div>整训戎旅。分二南之名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367077_comment'></div>创七德之筹谋。君无虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367077_comment'></div>臣无虚受。授受之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367077_comment'></div>任用匪轻。况全蜀奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367077_comment'></div>非贤勿守。方面重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367077_comment'></div>择善而从。顾臣庸愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367077_comment'></div>岂合祗拜。远奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367077_comment'></div>不敢逡巡。即以二月二日上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367077_comment'></div>天威在颜。风俗思变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367077_comment'></div>饮冰食蘖。策朽磨铅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367077_comment'></div>臣往在淮阳。已无展效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367077_comment'></div>出临彭蜀。又乏循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367077_comment'></div>虽圣恩不移。而微臣益惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367077_comment'></div>谨当宣扬皇化。镇抚蕃蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367077_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367077", 1367077, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>训率</span>吏兵。剪除夷獠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367077_comment'></div>庶冀毫发。增益山邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367077_comment'></div>陛下慎择任人。朝廷多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367077_comment'></div>伏愿更徵英彦。俾付西南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367077_comment'></div>许臣暮年。归侍丹阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367077_comment'></div>臣子之恳。君父之慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367077_comment'></div>天高听卑。下情上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367077_comment'></div>军府多事。税赋方殷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367077_comment'></div>臣今<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1367077", 1367077, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>逐便</span>指撝。乘閒式遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367077_comment'></div>救苍生之疲弊。宽陛下之忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367077_comment'></div>乃臣丹诚。缕缕于夙夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367077_comment'></div>无任悾之至。谨遣洋州司马摄参谋臣路球谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367077_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1367077_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　任剑南西川节度使，有上表。作品：《请入奏表》<div id='poem_1367082' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367082' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367082?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请入奏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367082")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367082_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367082'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367082'>右。自徐知道作乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367082_comment'></div>军府略空。救弊扶伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367082_comment'></div>事资安辑。臣夙夜陈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367082_comment'></div>起处不遑。伏以二陵攀号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367082_comment'></div>臣未修壤奠。万方有主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367082_comment'></div>臣未睹天颜。犬马之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367082_comment'></div>不胜恳。候士卒稍练。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367082_comment'></div>蕃夷渐宁。特望圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367082_comment'></div>许臣入奏。谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367082_comment'></div>伏听敕旨。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367082_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1367082_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　幕下有班宏，以处理疑难事立功。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　夏起，西川局势日趋紧急。高适专驻剑南西川节度辖区。东川置留后，由梓州刺史章彝充任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　秋至冬初，练兵备战，准备抗击吐蕃。时国势危殆，高适对政局极为愤懑。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4795b305e1114e29b60c4127d2375f96_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4795b305e1114e29b60c4127d2375f96");'><span id='4795b305e1114e29b60c4127d2375f96_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>，65岁</div><div id='4795b305e1114e29b60c4127d2375f96' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年1月</a>　正月，以严武为节度使，召高适回京，任刑部侍郎。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
安陆
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c1a341f216cc409883bd51c7e072d98b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c1a341f216cc409883bd51c7e072d98b");'><span id='c1a341f216cc409883bd51c7e072d98b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>，57岁</div><div id='c1a341f216cc409883bd51c7e072d98b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年12月24日</a>　玄宗以诸王分镇，适盛言不可，永王叛。肃宗召与计事，适判言永王且败，不足忧，肃宗奇之，除扬州大都督府长史、淮南节度使，讨永王李璘。年底，与韦陟、来瑱于安陆誓师。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州（江都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2bf8a29934cd456b817744e5d2d1b6c6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2bf8a29934cd456b817744e5d2d1b6c6");'><span id='2bf8a29934cd456b817744e5d2d1b6c6_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年2月</a>　二月，至扬州，有谢表。作品：《谢上淮南节度使表》<div id='poem_1367078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢上淮南节度使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（757年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367078_comment'></div>伏惟陛下大明照临。纯孝抚御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367078_comment'></div>汉主事亲之日。爰总六师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367078_comment'></div>轩后垂衣之辰。再清四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367078_comment'></div>犹以京华尚阻。国步暂艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367078_comment'></div>运黄石之神谋。推赤心于人腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367078_comment'></div>臣器非管乐。殊孔明之自比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367078_comment'></div>识谢孙吴。异山涛之暗合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367078_comment'></div>岂意圣私超等。荣宠荐臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367078_comment'></div>拔自周行。重寄方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367078_comment'></div>以时危而注意。窃愧非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367078_comment'></div>因国难以捐躯。顾为定分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367078_comment'></div>即当训练将卒。缉绥黎氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367078_comment'></div>外以平贼为心。内以安人为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367078_comment'></div>庶使殄灭凶丑。舞咏时邕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367078_comment'></div>报明主知臣之恩。成微臣许国之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367078_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1367078_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年2月</a>　二月，永王败死，高适兵尚未下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>　李白因从永王璘获罪，时系狱浔阳。有诗送张孟熊从军，张赴广陵见高适。高适对李白之厄难似无所帮助。<br /><a href="javascript: href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　春，仍驻扬州，登栖灵寺塔，有诗。作品：《登广陵栖灵寺塔》<div id='poem_45694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45694' class='poemTitle -----title
襄阳

-----title
彭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0e11d7f5836c44c19cd6025d0f7b9b54_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e11d7f5836c44c19cd6025d0f7b9b54");'><span id='0e11d7f5836c44c19cd6025d0f7b9b54_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　赴彭州任，一路山行，甚辛苦，有诗。作品：《赴彭州山行之作》<div id='poem_45563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴彭州山行之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45563")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_45563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45563'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45563'>峭壁连崆峒，攒峰叠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_45563", 45563, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>翠微</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45563'>鸟声堪驻马，林色可忘机。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45563'>怪石时侵径，轻萝乍拂衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45563'>路长愁作客，年老更思归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45563'>且悦岩峦胜，宁嗟意绪违。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45563'>山行应未尽，谁与玩芳菲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_45563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_45563'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_45563_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年6月</a>　六月初，到任彭州，有谢表。作品：《谢上彭州刺史表》<div id='poem_1367076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢上彭州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367076")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367076'>臣某言。伏奉圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367076_comment'></div>授臣彭州刺史。宠光自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367076_comment'></div>喜惧交集。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367076_comment'></div>臣本野人。匪求名达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367076_comment'></div>始自一尉。曾未十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367076_comment'></div>北使河湟。南出江汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367076_comment'></div>奉上皇非常之遇。蒙陛下特达之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367076_comment'></div>累登谏司。频历宪府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367076_comment'></div>比逆乱侵轶。淮楚震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367076_comment'></div>遂兼节制之权。空忝腹心之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367076_comment'></div>衔命感激。思效驽骀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367076_comment'></div>敢竭公忠。动无回避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367076_comment'></div>而智不周物。才难适时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367076_comment'></div>俄尘圣听。果速官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367076_comment'></div>实谓斧钺可待。流窜在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367076_comment'></div>陛下宏覆载之恩。明日月之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367076_comment'></div>始拜宫尹。今列藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367076_comment'></div>雨露之恩。更沾枯朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367076_comment'></div>阳和之气。忽振沈埋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367076_comment'></div>天高听卑。臣独何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367076_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。臣闻忠臣事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367076_comment'></div>虽死无贰。臣今未死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367076_comment'></div>敢忘至公。伏惟陛下哀臣愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367076_comment'></div>矜臣方直。臣虽在远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367076_comment'></div>若近天颜。臣以今月七日到所部上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367076_comment'></div>宣布德音。草木增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367076_comment'></div>敷陈睿泽。黎庶昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367076_comment'></div>无任悃屏营之至。谨附驿奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367076_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367076_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1367076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45598'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45598'>故人美酒胜浊醪，故人清词合风骚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45598'>杯中绿蚁吹转来，瓮上飞花拂还有。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45598'>前年持节将楚兵，去年<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_6_45598'>今年复拜二千石，盛夏五月西南行。<div id='poem_sentence_6_45598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_45598'>彭门剑门蜀山里，昨逢军人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_45598", 45598, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>劫夺</span>我。<div id='poem_sentence_7_45598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_45598'>到家但见妻与子，赖得饮君春酒数十杯，不然令我愁欲死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_45598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_45598'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(45598)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　杜甫于年底抵成都，高适闻讯后即寄诗问候。作品：《赠杜二拾遗》<div id='poem_45549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠杜二拾遗</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45549")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_45549_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45549'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(258, "poem_allusion_45549")'>草玄</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_45549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45549'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45549'>传道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_45549", 45549, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>招提客</span>，诗书自讨论。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45549'>佛香时入院，僧饭屡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_45549", 45549, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>过门</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45549'>听法还应难<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作说）</span>，寻经<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_45549", 45549, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>剩欲</span>翻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45549'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(258, "poem_sentence_3_45549")'>草玄</span>今已毕，此外复<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作后更）</span>何言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_45549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　奏上论“西山三城置戍”之疏，主张合东、西川为一道，罢西山三城之戍。作品：《请罢东川节度使疏》<div id='poem_1367085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢东川节度使疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_1367085")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367085'>剑南虽名东西两川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367085_comment'></div>其实一道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367085_comment'></div>自邛关黎雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367085_comment'></div>界于南蛮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367085_comment'></div>茂州而西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367085_comment'></div>经羌中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367085_comment'></div>至平戎数城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367085_comment'></div>界于吐蕃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367085_comment'></div>临边小郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367085_comment'></div>各举军戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367085_comment'></div>并取给于剑南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367085_comment'></div>其运粮戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367085_comment'></div>以全蜀之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367085_comment'></div>兼山南佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367085_comment'></div>而犹不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367085_comment'></div>今梓遂果阆等八州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367085_comment'></div>分为东川节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367085_comment'></div>岁月之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367085_comment'></div>西川不可得而参也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367085_comment'></div>而嘉陵比为夷獠所陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367085_comment'></div>今虽小定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367085_comment'></div>疮痍未平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367085_comment'></div>又一年已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367085_comment'></div>耕织都废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367085_comment'></div>而衣食之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367085_comment'></div>皆货易于成都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367085_comment'></div>则其人不可得而役明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367085_comment'></div>今可税赋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367085_comment'></div>成都彭蜀汉州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367085_comment'></div>又以四州残敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367085_comment'></div>当他十州之重役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367085_comment'></div>其于终久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367085_comment'></div>不亦至艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367085_comment'></div>又言利者穿凿万端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367085_comment'></div>皆取之百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367085_comment'></div>应差科者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367085_comment'></div>自朝至暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367085_comment'></div>案牍千重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367085_comment'></div>官吏相承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367085_comment'></div>惧干罪谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367085_comment'></div>或责之于邻保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367085_comment'></div>或威之以杖罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367085_comment'></div>督促不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367085_comment'></div>逋逃益滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367085_comment'></div>欲无流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367085_comment'></div>理不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367085_comment'></div>比日关中米贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367085_comment'></div>而衣冠士庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367085_comment'></div>颇亦出城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367085_comment'></div>山南剑南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367085_comment'></div>道路相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367085_comment'></div>村坊韨肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367085_comment'></div>与蜀人杂居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367085_comment'></div>其升合㪷储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367085_comment'></div>皆求于蜀人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367085_comment'></div>且田土疆界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367085_comment'></div>盖亦有涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367085_comment'></div>赋税差科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367085_comment'></div>乃无涯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367085_comment'></div>为蜀人之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367085_comment'></div>不亦难哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367085_comment'></div>今所界吐蕃城堡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367085_comment'></div>而疲于蜀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367085_comment'></div>不过平戎已西数城矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367085_comment'></div>邈在穷山之巅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367085_comment'></div>垂于险绝之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367085_comment'></div>运粮于束马之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367085_comment'></div>坐甲于无人之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367085_comment'></div>以戎狄言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367085_comment'></div>不足以利戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367085_comment'></div>以国家言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367085_comment'></div>不足以广土宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367085_comment'></div>奈何以险阻弹丸之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367085_comment'></div>而困于全蜀太平之人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367085_comment'></div>恐非今日之急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367085_comment'></div>国家若将已戍之地不可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367085_comment'></div>已镇之兵不可收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367085_comment'></div>当宜却停东川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367085_comment'></div>并力从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367085_comment'></div>犹恐狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367085_comment'></div>安可仰于成都彭蜀汉四州哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367085_comment'></div>虑乖圣朝洗荡关东扫清逆乱之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367085_comment'></div>傥蜀人复扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367085_comment'></div>岂不贻陛下之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367085_comment'></div>昔公孙宏愿罢西南夷临海专事朔方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367085_comment'></div>贾捐之请弃珠厓以宁中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367085_comment'></div>傥言政本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367085_comment'></div>匪一朝一夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367085_comment'></div>臣愚望罢东川节度以一剑南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367085_comment'></div>西山不急之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367085_comment'></div>稍以减削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367085_comment'></div>则事无穷顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367085_comment'></div>庶免倒悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367085_comment'></div>陛下若以微臣所陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367085_comment'></div>有裨万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367085_comment'></div>下宰相廷议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367085_comment'></div>降公忠大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367085_comment'></div>定其损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367085_comment'></div>与剑南节度终始处置。</div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1367085_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　秋，杜甫寄诗求助，高适当立即有所表示。<br /></div>
-----end

崇州（晋原）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年</a>　回蜀州，杜甫已先至，以诗迎之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年8月</a>　剑南兵马使徐知道反。高适于蜀州出兵，击徐知道。乱平，有贺表。作品：《贺斩逆贼徐知道表》<div id='poem_1367081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367081' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367081'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367081_comment'></div>臣闻人臣无将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367081_comment'></div>将必诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367081_comment'></div>逆贼前成都少尹兼侍御史伪称成都尹兼侍御史中丞剑南节度使徐知道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367081_comment'></div>中官携养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367081_comment'></div>莫知姓族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367081_comment'></div>荧惑主司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367081_comment'></div>叨窃宪台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367081_comment'></div>不能输沥肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367081_comment'></div>以答休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367081_comment'></div>而怀挟奸邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367081_comment'></div>啸聚同恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367081_comment'></div>倾竭府库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367081_comment'></div>涂炭黎氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367081_comment'></div>遂为欃枪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367081_comment'></div>恣行虿毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367081_comment'></div>杜塞剑道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367081_comment'></div>拥遏朝经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367081_comment'></div>部署凶残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367081_comment'></div>统领州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367081_comment'></div>曾未数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367081_comment'></div>荡坏一隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367081_comment'></div>郊原已空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367081_comment'></div>市井如扫。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367081_comment'></div>应接师旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367081_comment'></div>以今月二十三日大破贼众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367081_comment'></div>同恶翻然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367081_comment'></div>共杀知道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367081_comment'></div>大军庆快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367081_comment'></div>云物改容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367081_comment'></div>百姓欣欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367081_comment'></div>景色相贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367081_comment'></div>此皆社稷昭应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367081_comment'></div>神灵保持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367081_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下一德动天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367081_comment'></div>无远不届。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367081_comment'></div>兵戈向戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367081_comment'></div>华夏克宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367081_comment'></div>布萧王之赤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367081_comment'></div>竭臣子之丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367081_comment'></div>妖氛聚而皆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367081_comment'></div>郡国危而更安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367081_comment'></div>高视百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367081_comment'></div>能事斯毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367081_comment'></div>臣忝守藩翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367081_comment'></div>罹此艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367081_comment'></div>睹天地之廓清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367081_comment'></div>与飞动之咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367081_comment'></div>无任踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367081_comment'></div>谨奉表陈贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1367081_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
名山（百丈）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7b7c3a7c296e414f8eed0a191fddf638_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7b7c3a7c296e414f8eed0a191fddf638");'><span id='7b7c3a7c296e414f8eed0a191fddf638_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>，64岁</div><div id='7b7c3a7c296e414f8eed0a191fddf638' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　高适巡边至百丈，登百丈峰，有诗。作品：《登百丈峰二首》<div id='poem_45695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登百丈峰二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21646, "盛唐", "高适", "poem_title_45695")'>高适</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_45695'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_45695'>朝登百丈峰，遥望燕支道。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45695'>汉垒青冥间，胡天白如扫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45695'>忆昔霍将军，连年此<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作北）</span>征讨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45695'>匈奴终不灭，寒山徒草草。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45695'>唯见<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作有）</span>鸿雁飞，令人伤怀抱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_45695'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_45695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_45695'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(45695)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_45574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_45574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/45574?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_45574_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_45574'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' "poem_sentence_0_45574")'>晋武轻后事</span>，惠皇终已昏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_45574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_45574'>豺狼塞瀍洛，胡羯争乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_45574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_45574'>四海如鼎沸，五原徒自尊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_45574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_45574'>而今<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_45574", 45574, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>白庭</span>路，犹对青阳门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_45574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_45574'>朝市不足问，君臣随草根。<div id='poem_sentence_4_45574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
茂县（松州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a74d6e992b874c0f936d0146728c235f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a74d6e992b874c0f936d0146728c235f");'><span id='a74d6e992b874c0f936d0146728c235f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>，64岁</div><div id='a74d6e992b874c0f936d0146728c235f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　冬，攻吐蕃，作为关内主战场之侧翼，牵制吐蕃兵力，战败，松、维、保诸州陷落。<br /></div>
-----end
